wyldernes deſolate people called lāde albyon ye name ye eldyſt ſyſter called albyon yt deuyll takyng bodyes ye eyre man nature ī cōtreys ſhed poluſyō came lay thoſe woman begat thē horryble gyantꝭ cōtynued tyll ye cōmyng brute ſtory ſemeth meruaylous trewe though hath cōtynued englāde taken treuth amōge v englyſſhemen yet people therfore laugh v ſcorne ſo ſemeth may right well galfridus wrytith thyng men thynk yf trew wold haue put ī theyre cronycles well dyd thyngis laſſe meruell cōſyderyng touch ſpeke aſcanius siluius theyre chyldern became endyd ſuccedid thē kyngis alſo ōly affirmid ye ſeyd galfridus alſo diuers yt cōtrey gallia gretely inhabytid peple ye ſege troy lōg many yeris ye time ſuppoſid yt brute ſhuld enter land brytteyn wherefore diuers greate lernid men thynke lykely maner inpoſſible lande britteyn ſhulde ſo lōg deſolate people tyll tyme ſuppoſid comyng brute cōſideryng rokkis mounteyns douer ſo grete dayly opynly ſeen gallya ſo ſmall habytaciō therin ſuffer deſolate vnknowyn till comyng brute therfore ſome men day therbe theſe reſons dyuers take ſtory galfridꝰ feyned fable ſuppoſyng becauſe galfridus welchman born ſhuld fayn wors rule nat withſtandynge mayres preſence aſſauted ſtyll byſſhppes place longe tyme coude pacefyed wherof worde came byſſhop salyſburye beynge wyndeſore kynge meanes byſſhoppe caunterburye ſomewhat ſtyll contynued therfore ye citye made dyuers meanes obteyne fauour laſt meanes quene ſpecially one doctor grauyſende byſſhoppe london opteyned kynges fauour agayne receyued kyng citye made wyfe quene anne dyed buryed weſtmyſter ¶in xviii yere kynge rycharde hereſyes iohan wykelyffe began ſprynge englande becauſe ciſme ii pope ¶alſo xix yere kynge rycharde maryed iſabell doughter frenche many af souldyers caleys departed duke hooſt came kynge wherby duke companye ſore abaſſhed wherfore concluded flee leaue felde ſtandynge ben preſent duke departed ii ſonnes went fyrſt wale irelande erles salyſburye marche warwyke went deuynſhyre meanes one iohn̄ denham ſquyer gette ſhyppe ſayled gerneſey then vnto caleys ioyouſly receyued poſterne gate whan fyrſt departure theſe lordes knowen kynge lordes parte ſent coſte englande haue ſtopped late incontynent kynge diſpoyled towne lodlowe caſtell toke duches yorke anone kynge made ye duke somercetꝭ ſon ſlayne captayne caleys wherfore haſt went ouer haue taken caleys ye ſaid erles beynge kept hym wherfore yonge duke went toke guynes dayly many great aſſautes made betwene caleys guynes many men reſorted dayly came englande caleys ſocour lordes betauſe lacked money ſhyfted staple caleys xviii thouſande pounde ſende ouer ſayd mayſter iohn̄ denham great companye ſhyppes sandewyche wynne kynges nauey lyenge whiche ſo ſpedde hym toke towne toke lorde ryuers bedde toke lorde skalys toke many ſhyppes kynges nauey lyſt returned caleys nat without conſent many maryners whiche fauoured erle warwykethe kynges nauey takē ſande wyche sone kynge called parlyament couentrye ſayd duke yorke lordes attaynted treaſon theyr landes goodes ſeaſyd kynges vſe prouiſyon made yt man ſhulde paſſe ouer ſee vnto caleys nat withſtādyng comfort
